### 我的初步解释

- `CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping` 单独已经达到甚至略优于 full V2 的同一性能 regime，且 repeat bit-level stable。
- `StereoInitialization only` 仍然失败，说明 V2 的效果不是仅来自初始地图清理。
- `Full V2 minus NeedNewKeyFrame` 仍然强，说明 NeedNewKeyFrame 的巨大计数不是当前序列恢复的必要 gate。
- 因此 D²MA 的最小核心似乎可以定义为：在 `CreateNewKeyFrame` 阶段阻止 dynamic-depth RGB-D close points 创建静态 MapPoints，并在 `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints` 阶段阻止 dynamic instance feature pairs 通过 triangulation backdoor 进入静态地图。

### 本地文件

- gate ablation summary：`/home/lj/d-drive/Obsidian Vault/小论文/小论文2 动态改进Orb SLAM3/backend_map_admission_v2_gate_ablation_summary.csv`
- 实验记录：`/home/lj/d-drive/Obsidian Vault/小论文/小论文2 动态改进Orb SLAM3/动态改进Visual SLAM实验记录.md`

### 请重点回答

1. 现在是否可以把 D²MA 的最小方法定义收敛为 `CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping` 两个 static-map admission gate？
2. NeedNewKeyFrame gate 是否应该从主方法中移除，还是作为 optional safety guard 保留？
3. `StereoInitialization only` 失败是否足以反驳“只是初始地图清理带来收益”的质疑？
4. 下一步是否应停止同序列 2^4 gate 扫描，转向外部动态序列 sanity check？
5. 如果还补一个同序列消融，是 `CreateNewKeyFrame only` 更有价值，还是 `LocalMapping only` 更有价值？
6. 请给出更新后的论文方法段落和贡献表述，特别突出 D²MA 的最小机制。

## 答

根据 2026-05-13 的文档，我建议你**现在正式把 D²MA 收敛为 `CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping` 两个 static-map admission gate**。NeedNewKeyFrame gate 不应再放在主方法定义里；StereoInitialization only 的失败已经足够反驳“只是初始地图清理带来收益”；下一步应停止同一序列上的 2⁴ gate 扫描，转向外部动态序列验证。

## 1. D²MA 最小方法定义：可以收敛，但措辞要精确

当前最稳妥的定义是：

> **D²MA: Dynamic-Depth-Aware Map Admission**
> 在 ORB-SLAM3 RGB-D 的静态地图准入阶段，利用动态 mask 标记 dynamic-depth observations，并阻止这些观测在 `CreateNewKeyFrame` 和 `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints` 中被固化为静态 MapPoint。

这里的“最小”应理解为：

> **当前实验中已经验证的最小充分配置。**

不要写成：

> 已证明这两个 gate 是全局唯一必要配置。

因为你还没有跑 `CreateNewKeyFrame only` 和 `LocalMapping only`，所以严格数学意义上的 irreducible minimal set 还没完全证明。但从论文主线角度，已经足够把方法定义收敛到这两个 gate。

证据非常强：`CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping` 关闭了 stereo init 和 NeedNewKF，只保留两个地图准入 gate，仍达到 `ATE-SE3=0.017934`、`Sim3 scale=0.975517`、`matched=857`、final KFs/MPs=`224/3561`，并且 repeat 的 trajectory sha 与 KeyFrameTimeline sha 完全一致。相比 full V2 的 `ATE-SE3=0.018192`、scale=`0.972089`，它处于同一甚至略优的性能区间。

所以当前可以说：

> D²MA 的核心不是初始化清理，也不是 keyframe scheduling，而是 persistent static-map admission control。

这句话在实验记录里也已经形成了同样判断：`CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping` 是目前最强机制证据，核心恢复来自 persistent static-map admission control。

---

## 2. NeedNewKeyFrame gate：从主方法移除，作为 optional safety guard

NeedNewKeyFrame gate 的计数很大：full V2 中 `NeedNewKF dynamic close vetoed=119960`。如果只看计数，很容易误判它是关键 gate。但 gate ablation 已经直接证明：去掉它并不伤主结果。`Full V2 minus NeedNewKeyFrame` 达到 `ATE-SE3=0.017466`、`Sim3 scale=0.973968`、`matched=857`、final KFs/MPs=`223/3584`，并且 repeat bit-level 一致。

因此，NeedNewKeyFrame gate 不应该进入论文中的**最小主方法**。最稳妥表述是：

> We keep the keyframe-scheduling veto as an optional safety guard, but our gate-level ablation shows that it is not required for recovery on `freiburg3_walking_xyz`.

中文论文表述可以写成：

> 虽然 NeedNewKeyFrame 中的 dynamic close-point veto 触发次数很高，但去除此 gate 后系统仍保持同等精度和尺度一致性，因此本文将其归为辅助稳定项，而非 D²MA 的核心机制。

这样可以避免两个风险：

1. 方法定义被 reviewer 认为混入了 keyframe scheduling，而不是 map admission；
2. 你自己的主线又从“地图准入”被拉回“关键帧调度调参”。

我的建议：

```text
主方法 D²MA-min:
  CreateNewKeyFrame gate = on
  LocalMapping gate = on
  StereoInitialization gate = off
  NeedNewKeyFrame gate = off

完整工程配置 D²MA-full / D²MA-safe:
  CreateNewKeyFrame gate = on
  LocalMapping gate = on
  StereoInitialization gate = optional
  NeedNewKeyFrame gate = optional
```

论文主表用 D²MA-min。附录或扩展表报告 D²MA-full。

---

## 3. StereoInitialization only：足以反驳“只是初始化清理”

是的，足够反驳。

`StereoInitialization only` 的结果是 `ATE-SE3=0.602691`、`Sim3 scale=0.168261`、final KFs/MPs=`484/9873`。这个结果不只是“没有达到 V2”，而是几乎回到了 A raw RGB + raw depth 的失败 regime。

这说明：

```text
只清理初始地图
≠
阻止长期 dynamic-depth map contamination
```

论文里可以直接写：

> Initialization cleaning alone is insufficient. The stereo-initialization-only variant remains in the failure regime, with severe scale collapse and inflated map size. Therefore, the recovery of D²MA cannot be attributed merely to a cleaner initial map.

中文机制解释：

> walking_xyz 的主要病灶不是第一批初始 MapPoint 脏了以后全程带偏，而是动态 depth 在整个序列中不断通过 keyframe RGB-D close-point creation 和 LocalMapping triangulation 进入静态地图。初始化清理只能挡住早期入口，挡不住持续污染。

这个结论非常重要，因为它把 D²MA 从“初始化 trick”提升为“全序列地图准入机制”。

---

## 4. 下一步是否停止 2⁴ gate 扫描？应该停止

应该停止完整 2⁴ 扫描。现在继续做所有组合，边际收益很低，而且会稀释论文主线。

当前你已经回答了最关键的三个质疑：

1. **是否完整 V2 才有效？**
   不是。`CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping` 已经有效。

2. **是否只是初始化清理？**
   不是。`StereoInitialization only` 失败。

3. **NeedNewKeyFrame 的巨大计数是否必要？**
   不是。`Full V2 minus NeedNewKeyFrame` 仍然强。

这已经足以支持 D²MA 的主机制。实验记录也明确指出，下一步最缺的是外部动态序列 sanity check，而不是继续做同一序列上的 2⁴ 全组合扫描。

下一步优先级应改为：

```text
Priority 1:
  外部动态序列验证

Priority 2:
  一个同序列补充消融：CreateNewKeyFrame only

Priority 3:
  静态/低动态负例验证

Priority 4:
  mask 边界敏感性 / runtime / baseline 对比
```

---

## 5. 如果只补一个同序列消融：选 `CreateNewKeyFrame only`

我建议只补：

```text
CreateNewKeyFrame only
```

而不是 `LocalMapping only`。

原因是，在 ORB-SLAM3 RGB-D 中，`CreateNewKeyFrame` 更接近主污染入口：RGB-D close-depth candidate 可以直接被 unproject / admitted 为 MapPoint。`LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints` 更像 second-order backdoor：它阻止跨关键帧匹配对通过 triangulation 再进入地图。

如果 `CreateNewKeyFrame only` 已经接近 D²MA-min，那么你可以写：

> The direct RGB-D close-depth admission at keyframe creation is the dominant contamination path, while LocalMapping gate serves as a backdoor guard.

如果 `CreateNewKeyFrame only` 明显退化，而 `CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping` 很强，那么你可以写：

> Dynamic-depth contamination enters through both the direct RGB-D close-depth path and the LocalMapping triangulation backdoor; both gates are required for robust static-map admission.

`LocalMapping only` 的信息量较低，因为即使它有效性有限，也只是说明直接 RGB-D close-depth admission 没被关掉；这几乎是预期结果。实验记录中也已经建议，如果还做一个同序列补充，优先 `CreateNewKeyFrame only`，用于判断 LocalMapping backdoor 是否必要。

因此唯一推荐补充同序列实验是：

```text
D²MA-C only:
  StereoInitialization = 0
  NeedNewKeyFrame = 0
  CreateNewKeyFrame = 1
  LocalMapping = 0
```

判据：

```text
若 ATE-SE3 <= 0.025 且 scale >= 0.95:
  CreateNewKeyFrame 是主导 gate，LocalMapping 是安全补丁。

若 ATE-SE3 > 0.05 或 scale 明显下降:
  LocalMapping backdoor 是必要组成，D²MA-min 必须保留两个 gate。
```

---

## 6. 更新后的方法命名

继续用：

> **D²MA: Dynamic-Depth-Aware Map Admission**

不要改成 Dynamic Object-Aware Map Admission。

理由很简单：你的方法不是 object-level SLAM，不估计 object pose，不建 object landmarks，不做 object factor graph。dynamic object mask 只是 observation-level side-channel；真正被控制的是 **dynamic depth observation 是否能进入 static map**。

更准确的全名可以是：

> **D²MA: Dynamic-Depth-Aware Static Map Admission for RGB-D SLAM in Dynamic Scenes**

论文中首次出现时可以写：

> We call the proposed method D²MA, because it controls the admission of dynamic-depth observations into the persistent static map, rather than deleting RGB features or modifying pose-optimization weights.

中文表述：

> D²MA 不是动态物体建模方法，而是动态深度观测的静态地图准入控制方法。

这个命名还能自然区分你和 DynaSLAM / DS-SLAM / DynoSAM：

```text
DynaSLAM / DS-SLAM:
  semantic dynamic region removal / dynamic feature filtering

DynoSAM:
  dynamic object factor graph / object motion estimation

D²MA:
  dynamic-depth observation provenance + static-map admission veto
```

---

## 7. D²MA 最小机制的论文方法段落

可以这样写：

> **Dynamic-Depth-Aware Map Admission.**
> In RGB-D ORB-SLAM3, RGB features are associated with depth measurements and can be immediately converted into 3D MapPoints. In dynamic scenes, features on moving foreground objects may carry valid but dynamic depth. If these observations are admitted into the persistent static map, they become structurally inconsistent MapPoints and contaminate subsequent tracking, local mapping, and bundle adjustment.
>
> D²MA addresses this failure mode by using foundation-model dynamic masks only as a side-channel for static-map admission. It does not modify the RGB image, does not invalidate current-frame depth, and does not reweight pose-optimization residuals. Instead, it vetoes dynamic-depth observations at two persistent map admission points:
>
> 1. `CreateNewKeyFrame`, where RGB-D close-depth candidates would otherwise create static MapPoints;
> 2. `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints`, where dynamic instance feature pairs could enter the map through triangulation.
>
> This minimal admission policy prevents dynamic foreground depth from being converted into persistent static structure while preserving raw RGB-D sensing for short-term tracking.

中文版本：

> **动态深度感知地图准入。**
> 在 RGB-D ORB-SLAM3 中，RGB 特征点会与深度观测关联，并可直接反投影为三维 MapPoint。在动态场景中，落在运动前景上的特征点虽然具有有效深度，但该深度属于动态表面。如果这些 dynamic-depth observations 被接纳为长期静态地图点，就会形成结构性污染，进一步导致关键帧和地图点膨胀、路径长度异常与尺度一致性破坏。
>
> D²MA 不修改 RGB 图像，不直接 invalid 当前帧 depth，也不在 pose optimization 中做动态软权重；它仅将基础模型动态 mask 作为 side-channel，用于控制静态地图准入。具体而言，D²MA 在 `CreateNewKeyFrame` 阶段阻止 dynamic-depth RGB-D close points 创建静态 MapPoint，并在 `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints` 阶段阻止 dynamic instance feature pairs 通过三角化后门进入静态地图。
>
> 这一最小准入机制保留了 raw RGB-D tracking 的短期观测，同时切断动态深度进入长期静态地图的主要污染通道。

---

## 8. 更新后的贡献表述

建议贡献写成四点。

### Contribution 1：因果发现

> We conduct a causal RGB/depth intervention study and show that, for RGB-D ORB-SLAM3 on dynamic TUM walking sequences, the dominant failure source is not RGB appearance alone but dynamic foreground depth being admitted into the static map.

### Contribution 2：最小 D²MA 方法

> We propose D²MA, a dynamic-depth-aware map admission mechanism that uses foundation-model masks as side-channel signals to veto dynamic-depth observations at `CreateNewKeyFrame` and `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints`, without modifying RGB images, invalidating current-frame depth, or reweighting pose optimization.

### Contribution 3：gate-level ablation

> Gate-level ablation shows that the recovery is not due to initialization cleaning or keyframe scheduling. The minimal `CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping` admission gates recover the full V2 performance regime, while `StereoInitialization only` remains in the failure regime.

这个贡献有直接数据支撑：`CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping` 为 `ATE-SE3=0.017934`、scale=`0.975517`；`StereoInitialization only` 为 `ATE-SE3=0.602691`、scale=`0.168261`；`Full V2 minus NeedNewKeyFrame` 仍为 `ATE-SE3=0.017466`、scale=`0.973968`。

### Contribution 4：可复现实验协议

> We evaluate under a deterministic stable hybrid sequential protocol and report repeat trajectory and keyframe-timeline hashes to avoid misleading conclusions from ORB-SLAM3 backend scheduling nondeterminism.

这个贡献也很重要。你的记录已经说明此前 full 消融会受 ORB-SLAM3 前后端线程时序和关键帧插入分支影响；因此论文中报告 repeat statistics 是必要的，而不是装饰项。

---

## 9. 下一步实验路线

### 必做 1：外部动态序列 sanity check

现在最缺的是外部序列，不是更多 gate 组合。

优先级：

```text
TUM fr3/walking_rpy
TUM fr3/walking_halfsphere
TUM fr3/walking_static 或 sitting_xyz 作为低动态/负例
```

每条至少跑：

```text
A raw RGB + raw depth
C raw RGB + filtered depth  若有导出条件
D²MA-min: CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping
D²MA-full optional
```

判据不要要求都达到 `0.018m`，而是看趋势：

```text
D²MA-min 相比 raw:
  ATE-SE3 明显下降
  Sim3 scale 更接近 1
  final KFs/MPs 不再膨胀
  matched poses 不下降
```

### 必做 2：CreateNewKeyFrame only

这是唯一值得补的同序列 gate 消融。

它回答：

```text
LocalMapping backdoor 是否真的必要？
```

这会让方法段落更精确。

### 强烈建议：静态/低动态负例

如果 D²MA 在静态或低动态序列上伤害精度，会被 reviewer 抓住。你需要证明：

```text
在没有明显 dynamic-depth pollution 时，D²MA 不应显著减少有效静态 MapPoints；
ATE 不应明显恶化；
KFs/MPs 不应异常下降。
```

### 强烈建议：mask 边界敏感性

做最少三组：

```text
exact mask
erode radius=1
dilate radius=1
```

因为 D²MA 的核心是 admission veto，边界误差会直接影响是否误拒静态 MapPoint 或漏过动态 depth。

---

## 10. 现在论文主线可以这样收敛

你现在的主线已经非常清楚：

```text
dynamic depth pollution
→ persistent static-map admission contamination
→ keyframe / MapPoint inflation
→ scale drift and high SE3 ATE
→ D²MA admission veto at CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping
→ static map consistency restored
→ C/D-level ATE without RGB deletion or frame-level depth invalidation
```

更紧的版本：

> Dynamic masks are not used to delete visual evidence; they are used to prevent dynamic-depth observations from becoming static map structure.

这是你论文最该强调的一句话。

---

## 11. 当前最稳结论

最终判断如下：

1. **可以把 D²MA-min 定义为 `CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping`。**
   这是当前已验证的最小充分 static-map admission mechanism。

2. **NeedNewKeyFrame gate 从主方法移除。**
   保留为 optional safety guard 或 D²MA-full，不作为核心贡献。

3. **StereoInitialization only 的失败足够反驳初始化 trick 质疑。**
   结果仍在失败 regime，说明长期 map admission 才是关键。

4. **停止同序列 2⁴ gate 扫描。**
   只补 `CreateNewKeyFrame only`，然后转向外部动态序列。

5. **方法名继续用 D²MA: Dynamic-Depth-Aware Map Admission。**
   不要叫 Dynamic Object-Aware Map Admission，避免被误解为 object-level SLAM。

6. **论文创新点已经从“depth invalidation”升级为“static-map admission control”。**
   这比“只过滤 depth”更有论文价值，也更能解释为什么 V2 在不改当前帧 depth 的情况下恢复到 C/D 性能 regime。

# 七次问答

## 问

请基于我最新的外部序列验证结果，重新校准 D²MA 小论文路线。重点不是泛泛建议，而是判断：D²MA-min 是否仍适合作为主方法；如果外部动态序列上只部分改善，论文叙事应该如何收敛；下一步应优先补什么实验或机制。

## 当前方法定义

我已将方法收敛为：

```text
D²MA-min: Dynamic-Depth-Aware Map Admission
只在 ORB-SLAM3 RGB-D 的两个 persistent static-map admission gate 使用 dynamic-depth mask side-channel：
1. CreateNewKeyFrame: 阻止 dynamic-depth RGB-D close points 创建静态 MapPoint；
2. LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints: 阻止 dynamic instance feature pairs 通过 triangulation backdoor 进入静态地图。

不开启：
- StereoInitialization gate
- NeedNewKeyFrame gate
- frame-level dynamic depth invalidation
- RGB image filtering
- pose optimization soft weight/rejection
```

共同协议：

```text
profile = hybrid_sequential_semantic_only
maintenance_period = 4
ORB_SLAM3_MASK_MODE = off
STSLAM_FORCE_FILTER_DETECTED_DYNAMIC_FEATURES = 0
STSLAM_DYNAMIC_DEPTH_INVALIDATION = 0
raw RGB-D unchanged
mask/meta only as side-channel for map admission
```

## 已有主序列证据：walking_xyz

Early intervention 因果消融：

| case | RGB | depth | matched | ATE-SE3 | ATE-Sim3 | Sim3 scale | RPEt | RPER | final KFs | final MPs |
|---|---|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| A | raw | raw | 857 | 0.593504 | 0.254945 | 0.229283 | 0.019608 | 0.498886 | 478 | 10045 |
| C | raw | filtered | 857 | 0.018457 | 0.016026 | 0.970406 | 0.012053 | 0.371801 | 190 | 3302 |
| D | filtered | filtered | 857 | 0.018362 | 0.016258 | 0.972360 | 0.012353 | 0.368723 | 190 | 3750 |

D²MA gate-level result：

| case | StereoInit | NeedNewKF | CreateNewKF | LocalMapping | matched | ATE-SE3 | ATE-Sim3 | Sim3 scale | RPEt | RPER | final KFs | final MPs |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| Full V2 compat | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 857 | 0.018192 | 0.016019 | 0.972089 | 0.012130 | 0.372424 | 214 | 3592 |
| D²MA-min: CreateNewKF + LocalMapping | 0 | 0 | 1 | 1 | 857 | 0.017934 | 0.016274 | 0.975517 | 0.012161 | 0.367759 | 224 | 3561 |
| StereoInitialization only | 1 | 0 | 0 | 0 | 857 | 0.602691 | 0.280673 | 0.168261 | 0.019679 | 0.509767 | 484 | 9873 |
| Full V2 minus NeedNewKF | 1 | 0 | 1 | 1 | 857 | 0.017466 | 0.015513 | 0.973968 | 0.012085 | 0.384479 | 223 | 3584 |
| CreateNewKF only | 0 | 0 | 1 | 0 | 857 | 0.025601 | 0.024892 | 0.980431 | 0.013677 | 0.386654 | 217 | 3957 |

repeat：D²MA-min、Full V2 minus NeedNewKF、CreateNewKF only 均 trajectory sha 与 KeyFrameTimeline sha bit-level stable。

当前 walking_xyz 解释：

- dynamic depth pollution 是主因；
- CreateNewKeyFrame 是主导污染入口；
- LocalMapping 是必要 backdoor guard；
- NeedNewKF 不是核心；
- StereoInitialization only 足以反驳 initialization trick。

## 新增外部/低动态 sanity：walking_static

| raw baseline | run_1 | 906 | 0.997057 | 0.157951 | 0.084939 | 0.026161 | 0.626247 | 909 | 0 | 575 | 13872 |

- D²MA-min 对 raw failure 有可复现改善：ATE-SE3 0.997 -> 0.367，scale 0.085 -> 0.261，MPs 13872 -> 7331；
- 但它没有把外部动态相机序列拉回 walking_xyz 的强性能区间；
- has_pose/lost 完全一致，说明残余问题仍更像路径/尺度/地图污染，而不是 tracking lost；
- 这提示 D²MA-min 是有效机制，但可能不足以作为完整方法单独覆盖更强外部动态相机运动。

## 我希望你重点判断

1. 现在论文是否仍应把 D²MA-min 作为主方法？还是应调整为 “frontend depth support allocation + backend D²MA admission guard” 的双层方法？
2. walking_rpy 的部分改善但残余 failure，对论文是风险还是机会？应如何写，避免过度声称？
3. 是否应该补 `walking_halfsphere`，还是先做 walking_rpy failure diagnosis？
4. 下一步最值得做的最小实验是什么？我初步考虑：
   - walking_rpy 上跑 filtered-depth C / filtered RGB+depth D 上界；
   - walking_rpy 上跑 D²MA-min + backend dynamic depth invalidation/V1b；
   - 统计 walking_rpy 中被 veto 后仍进入 BA/local map 的污染路径；
   - mask boundary sensitivity；
   - 下载并跑 walking_halfsphere。
5. 如果目标是一篇可靠小论文，请给出新的主线排序：哪些是必须补，哪些是可选，哪些应停止。
6. 请重新给出论文贡献表述，尤其处理好 “walking_xyz 很强、walking_rpy 只部分改善” 这个不完美但真实的结果。

## 请输出

- 对当前证据强度的判断；
- 对 D²MA-min 主方法地位的判断；
- walking_rpy 残余失败的最可能原因排序；
- 下一步最小实验计划；
- 论文叙事与贡献表述；
- 需要避免的误区和审稿风险。

## 答
According to a document from 2026-05-13, my updated judgment is: **D²MA-min should remain the core backend method, but the paper should no longer sell it as a complete standalone solution for all dynamic RGB-D cases.** The safer mainline is:

> **Dynamic-depth contamination is a dominant static-map failure channel. D²MA-min is an effective, minimal backend admission guard for this channel. On harder motion sequences such as `walking_rpy`, it gives reproducible partial recovery but still requires either stronger depth-side front-end support allocation or additional failure-path handling.**

This keeps the contribution honest and still publishable.

### 1. Evidence strength after external validation

The evidence is now **stronger mechanistically but weaker as a universal performance claim**.

On `walking_xyz`, the causal chain is very strong. Raw RGB-D fails badly, filtered depth nearly recovers the best filtered RGB-D result, and D²MA-min reaches the same performance regime without RGB filtering or frame-level depth invalidation. The gate-level ablation also shows that `CreateNewKeyFrame` is the dominant pollution entrance, while `LocalMapping` is a real backdoor guard rather than decoration: `CreateNewKeyFrame only` gives `ATE-SE3=0.025601`, `scale=0.980431`, `final MPs=3957`; adding LocalMapping improves to `ATE-SE3=0.017934`, `scale=0.975517`, `final MPs=3561`.

The external validation changes the story. On `walking_static`, D²MA-min improves `ATE-SE3` from `0.043770` to `0.017037`, improves RPE, and reduces final KFs/MPs from `251/4419` to `183/2508`, with no lost frames. However, the Sim3 scale only rises from `0.328297` to `0.646556`, so it is useful as a low-dynamic sanity check, not as a full proof of scale recovery.

On `walking_rpy`, D²MA-min gives a large reproducible improvement but not full recovery: `ATE-SE3` improves from `0.997057` to `0.367386`, Sim3 scale from `0.084939` to `0.260907`, and final MPs from `13872` to `7331`; both runs are bit-level identical, and lost frames remain zero. This means the result is not async noise and not a tracking-lost issue, but the remaining error is still a serious path/scale/map-consistency failure.

So the evidence strength is:

| Claim                                                                  | Current support |
| ---------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------- |
| Dynamic depth pollution is a real dominant failure channel             | Strong          |
| D²MA-min is the right minimal backend mechanism on `walking_xyz`       | Strong          |
| `CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping` is a better definition than full V2 | Strong          |
| D²MA-min improves external dynamic sequences                           | Supported       |
| D²MA-min alone fully solves external dynamic RGB-D SLAM                | Not supported   |
| The paper should claim general SOTA dynamic RGB-D robustness           | Not yet         |

### 2. Should D²MA-min remain the main method?

Yes, but define its role carefully.

I would keep **D²MA-min** as the paper’s **core method**, not demote it to a minor ablation. The reason is that it is now well-isolated: it uses only two persistent static-map admission gates, keeps raw RGB-D unchanged, does not invalidate current-frame depth, does not delete RGB features, and does not reweight pose optimization. The uploaded prompt also states this exact method definition: `CreateNewKeyFrame` blocks dynamic-depth RGB-D close points from creating static MapPoints, while `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints` blocks dynamic instance pairs from entering the map through triangulation.

However, I would change the **paper framing** from:

> “D²MA solves dynamic RGB-D SLAM.”

to:

> “D²MA identifies and suppresses dynamic-depth static-map admission, a major but not exclusive failure channel in dynamic RGB-D ORB-SLAM3.”

That wording fits all three sequences:

* `walking_xyz`: D²MA-min nearly restores filtered-depth performance.
* `walking_static`: D²MA-min improves accuracy and map size without damaging tracking.
* `walking_rpy`: D²MA-min reproducibly suppresses part of the failure, but residual scale/path drift remains.

So the method remains central, but the contribution becomes **failure-channel isolation + minimal admission control**, not universal robustness.

### 3. Should the method become “frontend depth support allocation + backend D²MA admission guard”?

Not as the main method yet. Use it as the **next-stage full system hypothesis**.

The current paper can be organized as:

```text
Core method:
  D²MA-min = backend static-map admission guard.

Upper-bound / diagnostic front-end:
  filtered-depth C / filtered RGB-D D = early intervention oracle or front-end depth support allocation baseline.

Future or extended system:
  front-end depth support allocation + D²MA backend admission guard.
```

This separation is important. If you immediately redefine the main method as a two-layer front-end + backend system, the cleanest novelty of V2/D²MA gets blurred. The strongest scientific result is that **map admission alone can reproduce the strong regime on `walking_xyz` without changing input depth**. If you mix it too early with front-end filtering, reviewers may interpret the contribution as just “semantic depth masking again.”

But `walking_rpy` tells you that D²MA-min may not be sufficient for all motion regimes. Therefore, the next experimental question should be:

> Does `walking_rpy` fail because admission-only is intrinsically too late, or because the current mask/gate misses some dynamic-depth contamination path?

That question is better answered by upper-bound experiments before changing the method definition.

### 4. How to interpret `walking_rpy` partial improvement

`walking_rpy` is not a failure of the whole idea. It is a **mechanism boundary case**.

The positive part is substantial: D²MA-min reduces ATE by roughly 63%, improves scale, cuts final MPs almost in half, and remains bit-level reproducible. It also has zero lost frames, so the method is not creating a tracking coverage problem.

The negative part is equally important: `ATE-SE3=0.367386` and `scale=0.260907` are still in a residual failure regime, far from the `walking_xyz` result. The path diagnostics are especially telling: the raw arc ratio is `5.722309`, and D²MA-min still has raw arc ratio `5.292963`; Sim3-aligned arc ratio changes to `1.380969`, which suggests D²MA reduces map pollution but does not fully correct trajectory/path-length behavior.

The most likely explanation is:

> In `walking_rpy`, the dynamic-depth map-admission path is only one of several coupled failure channels. D²MA-min blocks many dynamic-depth candidates, but residual scale/path drift remains due to missed dynamic depth, mask boundary leakage, static support insufficiency under strong rotation, or dynamic observations that still affect tracking/local-map matching before admission.

This is actually a useful paper discussion point. It shows your method is not a black-box trick tuned to one sequence; it exposes where admission-only control is sufficient and where it is not.

### 5. Most likely causes of `walking_rpy` residual failure

#### 5.1 Missed dynamic-depth contamination before or outside the two D²MA gates

D²MA-min blocks `CreateNewKeyFrame` and `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints`, but it does not invalidate depth at the Frame level and does not affect all tracking/local-map uses of depth. On `walking_rpy`, the log still shows many accepted depth candidates: `275583` accepted at CreateNewKeyFrame, while `104743` were vetoed. If the mask misses boundaries, limbs, shadows, or moving-object depth near the boundary, enough dynamic depth may still enter as “static.”

#### 5.2 Stronger rotational camera motion changes the failure mode

`walking_xyz` is largely translational walking motion, while `walking_rpy` stresses rotational motion. ORB-SLAM3 RGB-D can keep producing poses with zero lost frames, but if static support is spatially weak or dynamic foreground occupies useful depth-rich regions, the path length can still drift. The fact that `walking_rpy` has no lost frames but large SE3/scale error points away from relocalization failure and toward accumulated map/path inconsistency.

#### 5.3 D²MA-min may suppress map pollution but not tracking-time dynamic influence

By design, D²MA-min does not delete RGB features, does not invalidate current-frame depth, and does not reweight pose optimization. That is methodologically clean, but it means dynamic observations can still influence short-term matching or local-map tracking before the map-admission veto. On `walking_xyz`, that was enough. On `walking_rpy`, it may not be.

#### 5.4 Mask quality / boundary sensitivity is now more important than on `walking_xyz`

The mean mask ratio for `walking_rpy` is reported as `0.113947`, and the runtime is about `532 ms/frame`. The method likely depends strongly on whether the dynamic person mask covers depth boundaries precisely enough. A one-pixel boundary leak can matter because RGB-D MapPoint creation happens at feature pixels, not semantic object interiors.

#### 5.5 Sequence association and evaluation coverage should be checked, but are probably not the main explanation

For `walking_rpy`, there are 909 valid association rows, no missing RGB/depth/mask, but 23 RGB-depth timestamp differences above `0.03s` and 3 GT time differences above `0.03s`. This is not enough to dismiss the experiment, but it should be reported as a data-quality caveat and checked with the same association policy across all variants.

### 6. What to do next: minimal experiment plan

#### 6.1 First priority: `walking_rpy` upper-bound C/D

Before adding mechanisms, run the same early-intervention upper bounds on `walking_rpy`:

```text
A_rpy: raw RGB + raw depth
C_rpy: raw RGB + filtered depth
D_rpy: filtered RGB + filtered depth
D²MA-min_rpy: raw RGB-D + map admission guard
```

This is the single most important next experiment.

Interpretation:

| Result                                   | Meaning                                                                                                                                      |
| ---------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| C/D recover near good scale and low ATE  | The front-end depth support allocation can solve `walking_rpy`; D²MA-min is too late or incomplete for this motion regime.                   |
| C/D only partially improve like D²MA-min | The issue is not just backend admission; mask quality, sequence association, or ORB-SLAM3 intrinsic failure under `walking_rpy` is involved. |
| C recovers but D²MA-min does not         | Dynamic depth must be suppressed before current-frame depth use, not only at map admission.                                                  |
| D recovers but C does not                | RGB feature support or appearance-level dynamic suppression becomes important under rotational motion.                                       |

This experiment directly decides whether the paper should remain “D²MA backend method” or expand to “front-end depth support allocation + D²MA guard.”

#### 6.2 Second priority: `walking_rpy` D²MA-min + V1b / frame-level invalidation

Run:

```text
D²MA-min only
V1b radius=1 only
D²MA-min + V1b radius=1
```

Goal: determine whether map admission and frame-level dynamic-depth invalidation are complementary.

Interpretation:

| Result                                  | Meaning                                                                                                                   |
| --------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| V1b or D²MA+V1b recovers scale strongly | Admission-only is too late for `walking_rpy`; current-frame dynamic depth use matters.                                    |
| D²MA+V1b is not better than D²MA        | Residual failure is not solved by simply invalidating masked depth; look at mask leakage, static support, or association. |
| V1b hurts but D²MA helps                | Admission guard is safer than early invalidation under rotational motion.                                                 |

This is more useful than immediately downloading another sequence, because it explains the current external failure.

#### 6.3 Third priority: failure-path statistics on `walking_rpy`

Add or extract per-frame/per-keyframe diagnostics:

```text
dynamic-depth candidates vetoed
accepted candidates near mask boundary
accepted depth candidates with high reprojection residual later
MapPoints accepted from boundary-risk pixels
MapPoints later used in BA
MapPoints later culled
per-frame delta_t_est / delta_t_gt
accumulated path ratio
local-map inliers before/after pose optimization
```

You already have aggregate counts, but aggregate counts cannot explain where the residual scale drift starts. The path diagnostics show the problem is not merely global ATE; it is trajectory arc/path inconsistency.

#### 6.4 Fourth priority: `walking_halfsphere`

Run it after the `walking_rpy` upper-bound experiment, not before.

`walking_halfsphere` will give broader external coverage, but it will not explain why `walking_rpy` remains in residual failure. If time is short, explanation is more valuable than another partially improved table.

### 7. Revised paper mainline

The mainline should now be:

```text
Observation:
  RGB-D ORB-SLAM3 in dynamic scenes can fail without losing tracking,
  because dynamic foreground depth is admitted into persistent static maps.

Causal evidence:
  On walking_xyz, depth-only filtering nearly matches full image-level filtering;
  dropout controls show this is not generic sparsification.

Method:
  D²MA-min vetoes dynamic-depth observations only at static-map admission gates:
  CreateNewKeyFrame and LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints.

Strong result:
  On walking_xyz, D²MA-min reaches filtered-depth performance regime.

External sanity:
  On walking_static and walking_rpy, D²MA-min improves ATE/RPE/map size
  with bit-level stable behavior and no lost frames.

Boundary:
  On walking_rpy, admission-only control leaves residual scale/path drift,
  indicating that dynamic-depth map admission is a major but not exhaustive
  failure channel.
```

This is a stronger, more honest paper than claiming SOTA on all dynamic scenes.

### 8. Updated contribution wording

I would write the contribution as follows.

#### Contribution 1: causal decomposition of RGB-D dynamic failure

> We decouple RGB appearance filtering from depth intervention and show that, in RGB-D ORB-SLAM3, dynamic foreground depth admitted into the static map is a dominant failure source. On `walking_xyz`, raw RGB-D suffers severe scale collapse and map inflation, while dynamic-depth intervention restores the filtered-depth performance regime.

#### Contribution 2: D²MA-min static-map admission guard

> We propose D²MA, a dynamic-depth-aware map admission mechanism that uses foundation-model masks only as a side-channel. D²MA does not modify RGB, does not invalidate current-frame depth, and does not reweight pose optimization. It vetoes dynamic-depth observations at `CreateNewKeyFrame` and `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints`, preventing dynamic foreground depth from becoming persistent static structure.

#### Contribution 3: gate-level isolation

> Gate-level ablation shows that `CreateNewKeyFrame` is the dominant admission entrance and `LocalMapping` is a necessary triangulation backdoor guard. `NeedNewKeyFrame` and `StereoInitialization` are not required for the core recovery.

This is backed by the gate results: full V2, D²MA-min, `StereoInitialization only`, `Full V2 minus NeedNewKF`, and `CreateNewKF only`, all with repeat-stable variants.

#### Contribution 4: reproducible external sanity with explicit limitation

> On external/low-dynamic and external dynamic TUM sequences, D²MA-min improves localization and map compactness without tracking loss, but `walking_rpy` reveals residual scale/path drift. We therefore characterize D²MA as a minimal admission guard for dynamic-depth map contamination, not a complete dynamic SLAM solution.

This contribution turns the imperfect `walking_rpy` result into a scientifically useful boundary condition rather than a hidden weakness.

### 9. What is must-have, recommended, optional, and should stop

#### Must-have

1. `walking_rpy` C/D upper-bound.
2. `walking_rpy` D²MA-min + V1b radius=1 or frame-level dynamic-depth invalidation.
3. Per-frame path/scale failure diagnostics for `walking_rpy`.
4. Same protocol table over `walking_xyz`, `walking_static`, `walking_rpy`.
5. Clear reporting of no RGB filtering, no depth invalidation, no pose soft weighting for D²MA-min.

#### Strongly recommended

1. `walking_halfsphere` after the `walking_rpy` diagnosis.
2. Mask boundary sensitivity on at least `walking_xyz` and `walking_rpy`.
3. Static or low-dynamic negative control beyond `walking_static`, such as `sitting_xyz` or `sitting_static`.
4. Runtime split: foundation-model mask generation versus backend overhead.
5. DynaSLAM / DS-SLAM-style semantic RGB-D baseline if reproducible in the same evaluator.

#### Optional

1. Full D²MA-safe with NeedNewKF gate as an engineering variant.
2. Qualitative map visualization showing dynamic-depth MapPoint suppression.
3. Pure monocular discussion or appendix.
4. More object-level dynamic modeling.

#### Stop or deprioritize

1. Full 2⁴ gate scanning on `walking_xyz`.
2. More `NeedNewKeyFrame` variants.
3. Pose optimization soft weighting / rejection as a main route.
4. RGB mask postfilter parameter sweeps as the main contribution.
5. Jumping to DynoSAM / SLAMMOT before the RGB-D depth-admission paper is stabilized.

### 10. Reviewer-risk framing

The biggest risk is overclaiming. Do not say:

> D²MA solves dynamic RGB-D SLAM.

Say:

> D²MA suppresses dynamic-depth static-map contamination and restores scale consistency when this channel dominates; external `walking_rpy` shows that stronger camera motion can still require earlier depth support allocation or additional contamination-path handling.

A second risk is method simplicity. The answer is: simplicity is acceptable because the novelty is causal isolation and correct SLAM-stage intervention, not architectural complexity.

A third risk is single-dataset overfitting. You now have `walking_static` and `walking_rpy`, but `walking_rpy` is only partial. To make the paper robust, add `walking_rpy` upper bounds and one more dynamic sequence if time allows.

A fourth risk is fairness. Make clear that D²MA-min keeps raw RGB-D unchanged, uses masks only as side-channel admission veto, and does not modify current-frame depth or pose residuals. That distinguishes it from image-level filtering and semantic depth deletion.

### 11. Final route decision

Keep **D²MA-min** as the core method.

But change the paper’s top-level title/concept from:

> “Robust Dynamic RGB-D SLAM with D²MA”

to something closer to:

> **D²MA: Diagnosing and Suppressing Dynamic-Depth Static-Map Admission in RGB-D SLAM**

or:

> **Dynamic-Depth Map Admission for Foundation-Model-Assisted RGB-D SLAM**

The paper’s honest claim should be:

> D²MA-min is a minimal, reproducible backend mechanism that blocks a major dynamic RGB-D failure channel. It can nearly recover the strong filtered-depth regime on `walking_xyz` and improves external sequences, but `walking_rpy` shows that admission-only control is not always sufficient. Therefore, the next full-system extension should combine front-end depth support allocation with D²MA backend admission guarding.

# 八次问答

## 问

请基于以下 D²MA-boundary / support-aware admission 初版结果，判断小论文方法路线是否应从 D²MA-min 扩展为 “D²MA-min + boundary-risk admission guard”，以及下一步是否应继续实现 delayed / multi-frame support-aware admission。

### 背景

此前 D²MA-min 定义为两个 static-map admission gate：

- `CreateNewKeyFrame`：阻止 direct dynamic-depth close points 创建静态 MapPoints；
- `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints`：阻止 dynamic instance feature pairs 通过 triangulation backdoor 进入静态地图。

在 `walking_xyz` 上 D²MA-min 接近 filtered-depth 强基线：

| method | matched | ATE-SE3 | ATE-Sim3 | scale | RPEt | RPER |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| D²MA-min | 857 | 0.017934 | 0.016274 | 0.975517 | 0.012161 | 0.367759 |

但在 `walking_rpy` 上只部分恢复：

| method | matched | ATE-SE3 | ATE-Sim3 | scale | RPEt | RPER |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| raw RGB-D | 906 | 0.997057 | 0.157951 | 0.084939 | 0.026161 | 0.626247 |
| D²MA-min | 906 | 0.367386 | 0.137205 | 0.260907 | 0.024261 | 0.591429 |
| C: raw RGB + filtered depth | 906 | 0.292579 | 0.125720 | 0.333615 | 0.023897 | 0.583789 |
| D: filtered RGB + filtered depth | 906 | 0.249133 | 0.123608 | 0.382943 | 0.025969 | 0.593776 |

### 机制诊断

对 `walking_rpy` 做 boundary admission diagnostic 后发现：

- D²MA-min 对 direct dynamic valid depth 有效：全序列约 `24.5%` 有效深度候选被 direct dynamic veto，前 200 帧约 `31.9%`。
- 但 direct dynamic veto 后仍存在 boundary leakage：前 200 帧 accepted depth candidates 中 `8.08%` 是 static feature 但 5px 内邻近 dynamic mask；新建 MapPoint 中这类点占 `13.13%`。
- 第 200 帧前累计创建 `2048` 个 static-near-mask MapPoints；此时系统已有 `131` KFs、`3888` MPs，estimated path `3.565893m`，早期路径膨胀已经形成。

因此我实现了 D²MA-boundary 初版。

### D²MA-boundary 初版实现

保持 raw RGB-D 不变、mask 只作为 side-channel、depth invalidation off。

新增规则：

- direct dynamic mask 内的候选仍由 D²MA-min hard veto；
- 对 static feature 但半径 `r` 内存在 dynamic mask support 的 close-depth candidate，不允许在 `CreateNewKeyFrame` 中直接创建新 MapPoint；
- 在 `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints` 中，若匹配对任一端特征是 static-near-dynamic-mask，则阻止该 pair 通过 triangulation backdoor 创建新 MapPoint。

这是 hard-veto 版本的 boundary-risk admission guard，还不是 delayed admission / multi-frame support 版本。

### 新结果

`walking_rpy` 半径敏感性：

| method | radius | matched | ATE-SE3 | ATE-Sim3 | scale | RPEt | RPER | skipped new boundary candidates | skipped LM boundary pairs |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| D²MA-boundary | 3 | 906 | 0.317809 | 0.130713 | 0.305339 | 0.027600 | 0.642786 | 5348 | 361 |
| D²MA-boundary | 5 | 906 | 0.269999 | 0.120722 | 0.361678 | 0.026173 | 0.606005 | 8179 | 587 |
| D²MA-boundary | 5 repeat | 906 | 0.269999 | 0.120722 | 0.361678 | 0.026173 | 0.606005 | 8179 | 587 |
| D²MA-boundary | 8 | 906 | 0.265845 | 0.120408 | 0.366495 | 0.033081 | 0.740172 | 10999 | 936 |

Sanity check：

| sequence | method | radius | matched | ATE-SE3 | ATE-Sim3 | scale | RPEt | RPER | final KFs | final MPs |
|---|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| walking_xyz | D²MA-boundary | 5 | 857 | 0.017884 | 0.016043 | 0.974357 | 0.011772 | 0.375444 | 176 | 3155 |
| walking_static | D²MA-boundary | 5 | 740 | 0.010972 | 0.008703 | 0.782028 | 0.010462 | 0.219777 | 141 | 1791 |

关键观察：

- `walking_rpy` 从 D²MA-min 的 `ATE-SE3=0.367386 / scale=0.260907` 提升到 `r5: 0.269999 / 0.361678`；`r8` 全局 ATE 和 scale 略好，但 RPE/RPER 更差。
- `r5` repeat bit-level stable。
- `walking_xyz` 没有退化，`walking_static` 反而继续改善。
- 但 `walking_rpy` 的 scale 仍远未恢复到 `walking_xyz` 强区间，因此 boundary hard-veto 只是明显缓解 residual failure，不是完整解决。

### 请重点回答

1. 这些结果是否足以把论文方法从 D²MA-min 扩展为两层：D²MA-min core + D²MA-boundary guard？
2. D²MA-boundary 应作为主方法的一部分，还是作为针对 mask-boundary uncertainty 的增强版/ablation？
3. `r=8` 全局 ATE 略好但 RPE/RPER 更差，是否说明 hard-veto 半径不应继续扩大，而应转向 delayed / support-aware admission？
4. 下一步最值得实现的是哪一种 support-aware 机制：multi-frame confirmation、local inlier support threshold、probationary MapPoint、还是 soft weighting / delayed promotion？
5. 论文叙事应该如何避免“又加了一个启发式边界 dilation”的质疑？
6. 请给出更新后的方法命名、贡献表述和下一轮实验清单。

## 答
According to a document from 2026-05-13，我的结论是：**可以把小论文方法从 D²MA-min 扩展为 “D²MA-min core + boundary-risk admission guard”，但现在还不能把它称为真正的 support-aware / delayed admission 方法。** 当前最稳妥的主方法应写成 **D²MA-B：Dynamic-Depth-Aware Map Admission with Boundary-Risk Guard**；D²MA-min 作为核心机制和必要消融，D²MA-boundary r=5 作为当前完整方法。下一步不应继续扩大 hard-veto 半径，而应转向 **probationary / delayed map admission**。

### 1. 总判断

这轮结果把 `walking_rpy` 的残余 failure 解释得更清楚了。之前 D²MA-min 只堵住了“特征点直接落在 dynamic mask 内”的动态深度污染，但没有处理 mask 边缘的混合深度、遮挡边界和实例分割边界误差。你的诊断显示，D²MA-min 后前 200 帧 accepted depth candidates 中仍有 `8.08%` 是 static feature 但 5px 内邻近 dynamic mask，新建 MapPoint 中这类点占 `13.13%`，并且第 200 帧前已经累计创建 `2048` 个 static-near-mask MapPoints；此时系统已有 `131` KFs、`3888` MPs，estimated path 已到 `3.565893m`，说明路径膨胀早期已经形成。

这不是“随便加一个 dilation 半径”的证据，而是一个具体污染通道：**dynamic-depth contamination 通过 mask boundary / mixed-depth uncertainty 绕过了 D²MA-min 的 direct dynamic veto。**

因此，D²MA-boundary 有资格进入主方法，而不是只作为无关小消融。但它应该被表述为：

> D²MA 的第二层 boundary-risk admission guard，用于处理 dynamic mask 边界附近的 RGB-D association uncertainty。

不要表述为：

> 我们把 mask 膨胀了一圈再删点。

这两种说法的审稿观感完全不同。

### 2. 是否应从 D²MA-min 扩展为 D²MA-min + boundary-risk guard

应该扩展。

理由有三点。

第一，`walking_rpy` 上收益明确。D²MA-min 是 `ATE-SE3=0.367386`、scale=`0.260907`；D²MA-boundary r=5 提升到 `ATE-SE3=0.269999`、scale=`0.361678`，相当于在 D²MA-min 基础上又明显削弱了残余 scale/path failure。r=5 还 repeat bit-level stable。

第二，boundary guard 没有破坏主序列和低动态 sanity。`walking_xyz` 上 r=5 是 `ATE-SE3=0.017884`、scale=`0.974357`，与 D²MA-min / filtered-depth 强区间一致；`walking_static` 上 r=5 是 `ATE-SE3=0.010972`、scale=`0.782028`，也没有出现“过删导致崩溃”的负面现象。

第三，r=5 的机制位置仍然符合 D²MA 的核心哲学：raw RGB-D 不变，depth invalidation off，mask 只作为 side-channel，不在 pose optimization 做 soft weight/rejection，只在 static-map admission gate 上阻止高风险 dynamic-depth observations 固化为长期静态 MapPoint。这个边界 guard 没有把你带回旧的“tracking 阶段删点/降权”失败路线。

所以论文里的方法层次建议是：

```text
D²MA-min:
  Direct dynamic-depth admission veto
  Gates: CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping

D²MA-B / D²MA-boundary:
  D²MA-min
  + boundary-risk admission guard for static-near-dynamic-mask depth candidates
  Default radius: r = 5 px
```

D²MA-min 不应被丢掉。它是证明“dynamic-depth static-map admission 是主要失败通道”的核心机制。D²MA-B 是当前更强、更完整的工程方法。

### 3. D²MA-boundary 是主方法，还是增强版/ablation

我的建议是：**D²MA-B 作为主方法，D²MA-min 作为核心 ablation。**

原因是你现在已经不只是想证明 D²MA-min 在 `walking_xyz` 好，而是要面对 `walking_rpy` 这种更难外部动态序列。D²MA-min 在 `walking_rpy` 只部分恢复，D²MA-B r=5 把结果从 `0.367386` 推到 `0.269999`，已经接近 filtered-depth C 的 `0.292579`，并进一步接近 filtered RGB+depth D 的 `0.249133`。你之前的上界实验也表明，`walking_rpy` 即使用 C/D 也不能像 `walking_xyz` 那样恢复到 `0.018m`，所以 r=5 其实已经非常接近当前输入级上界区间。

论文主表可以这样组织：

```text
Raw ORB-SLAM3 RGB-D
Filtered-depth C
Filtered RGB-D D
D²MA-min
D²MA-B r=5
```

其中：

* D²MA-min 证明核心 admission hypothesis；
* D²MA-B r=5 作为最终方法；
* C/D 是 early-intervention upper-bound，不是你的最终 backend 方法；
* r=3/r=8 放入 sensitivity table。

不要把 D²MA-boundary 只放在 appendix。它解决的是 `walking_rpy` 上 D²MA-min 暴露出来的核心残余污染通道，已经属于方法主体。

### 4. 如何解释 r=8：不要继续扩大 hard-veto 半径

`r=8` 的全局 ATE 和 scale 略优于 r=5：`0.265845` vs `0.269999`，scale `0.366495` vs `0.361678`。但这个提升非常小，而 RPEt/RPER 明显变差：RPEt 从 r=5 的 `0.026173` 升到 `0.033081`，RPER 从 `0.606005` 升到 `0.740172`。

这说明 r=8 很可能已经进入了 **over-veto / support starvation** 的边界。它可能通过删除更多边界污染点略微改善全局轨迹对齐，但同时牺牲了局部连续性、局部地图支撑或短期 tracking support。

论文里应这样表述：

> Increasing the boundary radius beyond 5 px yields marginal global ATE improvement but significantly worsens local RPE, suggesting that hard boundary veto cannot be safely scaled by simply enlarging the radius. This motivates a delayed or support-aware admission strategy rather than more aggressive mask dilation.

中文更直接：

> r=8 不是更好的主配置，而是 hard-veto 的上限信号。它告诉我们：继续扩大半径不是正确路线，应该把 boundary-risk candidate 从“立即 hard veto”升级为“延迟准入 / 跨帧确认”。

所以默认配置应选 r=5。r=8 作为证据放进 sensitivity table，用来支撑“不能继续粗暴扩大边界”的论点。

### 5. 下一步最值得实现的 support-aware 机制

最值得做的是：

> **Probationary MapPoint + delayed promotion**

也就是把 boundary-risk candidate 从“立即创建静态 MapPoint”改为“候选观察 / probationary point”，等跨帧静态支持足够后再晋升为正式 MapPoint。

优先级如下。

#### 5.1 第一优先：probationary MapPoint / delayed promotion

这是最符合你当前发现的机制。

D²MA-boundary hard-veto 的问题是二元判断过硬：

```text
inside dynamic mask -> veto
near dynamic mask -> veto
else -> admit
```

但真实情况更复杂。boundary-risk 点可能有三类：

```text
真正动态边界点：应拒绝
静态背景但靠近人体边界：应保留
混合深度/遮挡边界：短期不可信，需要观察
```

因此最合理的机制是：

```text
safe static candidate:
  立即按 ORB-SLAM3 原逻辑创建 MapPoint

direct dynamic candidate:
  hard veto

boundary-risk candidate:
  不立即创建正式静态 MapPoint
  进入 probation buffer
  满足跨帧静态支持后再 promotion
  否则 discard
```

建议最小实现：

```text
boundary_risk if:
  feature outside dynamic mask
  but within r=5 px of dynamic mask

probationary candidate stores:
  keyframe id
  feature index
  depth
  mask distance
  semantic/instance id nearby
  reprojection residual history
  observed frame count
  outside-mask confirmation count
  static-neighbor support count
```

promotion 条件第一版不要复杂：

```text
promote if:
  observed in >= 2 keyframes
  and not inside dynamic mask in later observations
  and reprojection residual passes normal ORB-SLAM3 threshold
  and depth consistency is stable
  and local static support is sufficient

discard if:
  repeatedly near/inside dynamic mask
  or high residual
  or fails to match in following keyframes
```

这个机制比继续 r=8/r=10 有论文价值，因为它把“边界不确定性”从一个膨胀半径问题变成了 **temporal evidence accumulation / delayed static-map admission** 问题。

#### 5.2 第二优先：local static support threshold

这个机制应作为 delayed promotion 的辅助条件，而不是单独主方法。

可以定义：

```text
local_static_support = number of safe static inliers / accepted static MapPoints
                       within image grid cell or local neighborhood
```

使用方式：

```text
if boundary-risk candidate has weak local static support:
    do not promote
if global/static support is already weak:
    do not hard delete more; keep in probation instead of immediate veto
```

这个 guard 的意义是防止 r=8 那种过度 veto 导致局部 tracking support 变差。它不是动态判断本身，而是 **admission safety check**。

#### 5.3 第三优先：multi-frame confirmation

multi-frame confirmation 很重要，但它最好作为 probationary promotion 的判断条件，而不是另做一个独立模块。

例如：

```text
confirm_static if:
  boundary-risk point is observed outside dynamic mask in >= 2 later keyframes
  and residual remains low
  and associated depth remains consistent
```

它回答的是：

> 这个边界点是否真的属于静态背景，而不是一次性边界混合深度？

#### 5.4 不建议：pose soft weighting

不要把下一步做成 soft weighting。你历史实验已经多次显示 track-local-map / pose optimization 软降权容易造成稳定负收益。当前 D²MA 的优势恰恰是“不碰 pose optimization，不删 tracking support，只管静态地图准入”。

如果需要 soft 的概念，应限定在 admission score / promotion score，而不是 pose residual weight。

### 6. 如何避免“只是启发式边界 dilation”的质疑

你需要把 boundary guard 解释成 RGB-D depth association uncertainty，而不是 mask dilation。

审稿人会质疑：

> 你是不是就是把 mask 膨胀 5px，然后删更多点？

你的回答应分三层。

第一，动机不是任意 dilation，而是诊断出来的边界污染通道。D²MA-min 后仍有大量 static-near-mask MapPoints 早期进入地图，第 200 帧前已经有 `2048` 个这类 MapPoints，且路径膨胀已经形成；这说明 boundary-risk 不是随便猜的，而是由 MapPoint provenance 统计发现的污染路径。

第二，操作位置不是 RGB mask filtering，而是 static-map admission。你没有删除 RGB 图像，没有 invalid 当前帧 depth，没有在 tracking pose optimization 降权；你只是在 `CreateNewKeyFrame` 和 `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints` 上阻止 boundary-risk depth 直接变成长期静态 MapPoint。

第三，r=8 的结果反而证明“越大越好”不成立。r=8 ATE 略好但 RPE/RPER 明显变差，所以你的结论不是“更大 mask 更好”，而是“hard boundary veto 有上限，需要 delayed/support-aware admission”。

论文里可以直接写：

> Boundary-risk admission is not used as image-level mask dilation. It is applied only to RGB-D map admission, motivated by observed static-near-mask MapPoint contamination. The radius sensitivity further shows that aggressive hard vetoing degrades local consistency, motivating delayed admission rather than larger masks.

### 7. 更新后的方法命名

建议用这个层级：

```text
D²MA:
  Dynamic-Depth-Aware Map Admission
  总方法家族名称

D²MA-min:
  Direct dynamic-depth map admission veto
  gates = CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping

D²MA-B:
  D²MA with Boundary-Risk Admission Guard
  D²MA-min + static-near-dynamic-mask candidate guard

D²MA-DA:
  D²MA with Delayed Admission
  下一阶段待验证版本
```

当前论文主方法可以叫：

> **D²MA-B: Boundary-Risk Dynamic-Depth Map Admission for RGB-D SLAM in Dynamic Scenes**

如果你想标题更简洁：

> **D²MA: Dynamic-Depth-Aware Map Admission with Boundary-Risk Guard**

方法段落中要明确：

```text
D²MA-B keeps raw RGB-D unchanged.
It does not perform image-level RGB filtering.
It does not invalidate current-frame depth.
It does not reweight pose optimization.
It only controls whether dynamic or boundary-risk depth observations are admitted into persistent static map structures.
```

### 8. 更新后的贡献表述

建议贡献写成四点。

#### 8.1 贡献一：动态深度准入污染的因果分解

> We show that dynamic foreground depth admitted into the persistent static map is a dominant failure channel for RGB-D ORB-SLAM3 in dynamic scenes. On `walking_xyz`, depth-only intervention recovers the strong filtered RGB-D regime, while RGB-only filtering remains insufficient.

#### 8.2 贡献二：D²MA-min：静态地图准入核心机制

> We propose D²MA-min, a minimal dynamic-depth-aware admission mechanism that vetoes dynamic-depth observations at `CreateNewKeyFrame` and `LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints`, without RGB filtering, frame-level depth invalidation, or pose-level soft weighting.

#### 8.3 贡献三：boundary-risk admission guard

> We identify a residual mask-boundary leakage path in `walking_rpy`, where static-labeled features near dynamic masks still create contaminated MapPoints. We introduce D²MA-B, a boundary-risk admission guard that prevents static-near-dynamic-mask depth observations from immediately entering the persistent static map.

#### 8.4 贡献四：失败边界与 delayed admission 方向

> Radius sensitivity shows that larger hard-veto regions can improve global ATE only marginally while worsening local RPE, revealing the limitation of hard boundary veto and motivating support-aware delayed map admission.

这第四点很重要。它让 r=8 的“不完美”变成论文价值，而不是缺陷。

### 9. 下一轮最小实验清单

#### 9.1 必做：D²MA-B r=5 在另一条动态序列上的验证

现在 `walking_xyz`、`walking_rpy`、`walking_static` 已经不错，但如果要写小论文，最好补 `walking_halfsphere` 或另一个 TUM dynamic sequence。

最小表格：

```text
raw RGB-D
D²MA-min
D²MA-B r=5
filtered-depth C if available
filtered RGB-D D if available
```

成功判据：

```text
D²MA-B 相比 D²MA-min:
  ATE-SE3 更低
  scale 更接近 1
  final KFs/MPs 不膨胀
  matched 不下降
  RPE 不显著恶化
```

如果 `walking_halfsphere` 只部分改善，也不是失败；你可以把它作为 “boundary-aware admission helps but does not solve all dynamic camera motions” 的外部验证。

#### 9.2 必做：same-count non-boundary veto control

为了避免“你只是删了更多点”的质疑，建议做一个 cheap control：

```text
D²MA-min + random static candidate veto
数量匹配 D²MA-B r=5 的 skipped new boundary candidates
但 veto 对象从非 boundary static candidates 中随机采样
```

或者：

```text
D²MA-min + far-from-mask static veto
veto 数量与 boundary r=5 相同
但对象距离 dynamic mask > 20 px
```

如果这个 control 不能达到 r=5 的效果，就能证明 D²MA-B 的收益来自 **near-mask boundary-risk targeting**，不是来自普通 map sparsification。

这是非常有论文价值的补充实验。

#### 9.3 强烈建议：D²MA-DA delayed admission 原型

不要一开始做复杂多状态系统。第一版只做最小 delayed admission：

```text
direct dynamic:
  hard veto

safe static:
  normal admission

boundary-risk:
  no immediate MapPoint creation
  save probation candidate
  promote after 2 keyframe observations if residual/depth/mask status stable
```

比较：

```text
D²MA-min
D²MA-B r=5 hard-veto
D²MA-DA r=5 delayed admission
D²MA-B r=8 hard-veto
```

成功判据：

```text
walking_rpy:
  ATE-SE3 <= r5 hard-veto
  scale >= r5 hard-veto
  RPEt/RPER <= r5 hard-veto
  final KFs/MPs 不膨胀

walking_xyz/static:
  不退化
```

如果 D²MA-DA 的 ATE 不比 r5 好，但 RPE 明显更稳，也有价值：说明 delayed admission 缓解了 hard-veto 的局部支持损伤。

#### 9.4 可选：boundary gate split

如果还有时间，再拆：

```text
CreateNewKeyFrame boundary only
LocalMapping boundary only
CreateNewKeyFrame + LocalMapping boundary
```

但这不是第一优先级。你已经有 D²MA-min 的 gate-level 证据，当前更重要的是证明 boundary guard 不是泛化差的半径启发式。

### 10. 当前论文主线应如何收敛

建议主线更新为：

```text
Observation:
  RGB-D ORB-SLAM3 in dynamic scenes can fail without tracking lost,
  because dynamic foreground depth is admitted into persistent static maps.

Core mechanism:
  D²MA-min blocks direct dynamic-depth observations at static-map admission gates.

External residual:
  On walking_rpy, D²MA-min improves raw failure but residual scale/path drift remains.

Diagnosis:
  Boundary leakage remains: static-labeled features near dynamic masks create many MapPoints early.

Method extension:
  D²MA-B adds boundary-risk admission guard at the same map-admission gates.

Result:
  D²MA-B improves walking_rpy from D²MA-min 0.367/scale 0.261 to r5 0.270/scale 0.362,
  while preserving walking_xyz and walking_static sanity.

Limitation:
  Larger hard-veto radius worsens local RPE, so future direction is delayed/support-aware admission.
```

这条线比“D²MA-min 在 xyz 很强，但 rpy 不够强”更完整，因为你已经找到了 rpy 残余 failure 的一条具体路径，并且用 D²MA-B 初步缓解了它。

### 11. 当前最稳的论文定位

不要写：

> D²MA solves dynamic RGB-D SLAM.

也不要写：

> Boundary dilation fixes `walking_rpy`.

应写：

> D²MA identifies dynamic-depth static-map admission as a major failure channel in RGB-D ORB-SLAM3. D²MA-min blocks direct dynamic-depth admission, while D²MA-B further handles boundary-risk depth observations caused by mask-edge and mixed-depth uncertainty. Experiments show that this staged admission strategy restores the strong regime on `walking_xyz`, improves low-dynamic sanity, and significantly reduces residual failure on `walking_rpy`, though hard boundary veto still has limits under stronger camera motion.

中文版本：

> 本文不是提出一个通用动态物体删除器，而是提出一个动态深度观测的静态地图准入控制机制。D²MA-min 切断 mask 内动态深度的直接建图通道，D²MA-B 进一步处理 mask 边界附近的混合深度和遮挡边界污染。实验表明，该机制能在 `walking_xyz` 上恢复强基线，在 `walking_static` 上不破坏系统，并在更困难的 `walking_rpy` 上显著缓解残余尺度/路径漂移；但 hard-veto 半径不能无限扩大，后续应转向 delayed/support-aware admission。

### 12. 最终路线建议

当前最推荐路线是：

```text
Main method:
  D²MA-B r=5

Core ablation:
  D²MA-min

Sensitivity:
  r=3 / r=5 / r=8

Control:
  same-count non-boundary veto

Next mechanism:
  D²MA-DA probationary delayed admission

External validation:
  walking_halfsphere or another TUM dynamic sequence
```

如果时间很紧，优先级是：

```text
1. same-count non-boundary veto control
2. walking_halfsphere D²MA-min / D²MA-B r=5
3. D²MA-DA minimal prototype on walking_rpy
```

我的最终判断是：**D²MA-boundary r=5 现在已经值得进入主方法；r=8 的结果明确说明不要继续扩大 hard-veto 半径；下一步最有价值的创新不是更大 boundary，而是 boundary-risk candidate 的 probationary / delayed static-map admission。**

# 九次问答

## 问

我们按照你上一轮建议完成了两项关键补充实验：same-count non-boundary veto control，以及 `fr3/walking_halfsphere` 外部动态序列验证。请你基于以下结果继续判断论文主线是否应正式收敛为 D²MA-min + D²MA-Boundary r5，并给出下一步 D²MA-DA / delayed admission 的最小实现路线。

### 1. same-count non-boundary veto control

目的：排除 D²MA-B r5 的收益只是来自“删点更多 / 地图更稀疏”的可能性。

实现：D²MA-min direct dynamic gates 保持开启，但 boundary targeting 关闭；系统先统计如果启用 D²MA-B r5 会跳过多少 boundary-risk candidate，然后改为跳过同数量的 non-boundary static candidate。

结果：

| sequence | method | matched | ATE-SE3 | ATE-Sim3 | Sim3 scale | RPEt | RPER | final KFs | final MPs |
|---|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| walking_rpy | raw RGB-D | 906 | 0.997057 | 0.157951 | 0.084939 | 0.026161 | 0.626247 | 909 | 13872 |
| walking_rpy | D²MA-min | 906 | 0.367386 | 0.137205 | 0.260907 | 0.024261 | 0.591429 | 426 | 7331 |
| walking_rpy | D²MA-B r5 | 906 | 0.269999 | 0.120722 | 0.361678 | 0.026173 | 0.606005 | 370 | 6006 |
| walking_rpy | same-count non-boundary control r5 | 906 | 0.604425 | 0.156306 | 0.138884 | 0.025395 | 0.593053 | 427 | 7389 |

control 计数：

| metric | value |
|---|---:|
| boundary budget new candidates | 7990 |
| skipped non-boundary new candidates | 7988 |
| boundary budget LM pairs | 246 |
| skipped non-boundary LM pairs | 209 |

初步解读：同量删除 non-boundary candidates 不但不能复现 D²MA-B r5，反而明显差于 D²MA-min。这支持 D²MA-B 的收益来自 near-mask boundary-risk targeting，而不是 generic sparsification。

### 2. `fr3/walking_halfsphere` 外部动态验证

数据处理：下载 TUM RGB-D `fr3/walking_halfsphere`，保持 raw RGB-D，不使用 filtered depth；用当前 YOLOE/SAM3 配置生成 mask side-channel。文件存在性检查通过，但原始 association 存在 26 个 `rgb_depth_time_diff>0.03` 和 3 个 `gt_time_diff>0.03`，三组方法使用完全相同 association。

前端 mask 统计：

| item | value |
|---|---:|
| exported frames | 1067 |
| mean mask ratio | 0.129538 |
| mean filtered detections | 1.10684 |
| mean motion | 0.43566 |
| mean geometry dynamic | 0.42473 |

后端结果：

| sequence | method | matched | ATE-SE3 | ATE-Sim3 | Sim3 scale | RPEt | RPER | final KFs | final MPs | final path |
|---|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| walking_halfsphere | raw RGB-D | 1064 | 0.418817 | 0.278236 | 0.560136 | 0.020018 | 0.521662 | 610 | 13213 | 18.488295 |
| walking_halfsphere | D²MA-min | 1064 | 0.178466 | 0.133784 | 0.798252 | 0.016987 | 0.498543 | 370 | 5491 | 16.107576 |
| walking_halfsphere | D²MA-B r5 | 1064 | 0.156093 | 0.118844 | 0.823258 | 0.016220 | 0.484402 | 308 | 4804 | 15.225326 |

gate 统计：

| method | direct new veto | LM instance pairs skipped | boundary skipped new | boundary LM pairs skipped |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| D²MA-min | 131112 | 3054 | 0 | 0 |
| D²MA-B r5 | 133793 | 3516 | 8502 | 529 |

初步解读：在外部动态人物序列上，D²MA-min 相比 raw baseline 显著改善；D²MA-B r5 又继续优于 D²MA-min，并且 RPEt/RPER 同步下降，没有表现出 r8 那种局部连续性恶化。

### 3. 目前论文叙事候选

我们倾向于将主线收敛为：

```text
D²MA-min:
  Direct dynamic depth / instance-bound feature 不进入长期静态地图。

D²MA-B:
  在 D²MA-min 之上加入 boundary-risk admission guard，处理 mask boundary、mixed depth、occlusion edge 带来的伪静态地图污染。

D²MA-DA:
  下一步把 hard boundary veto 升级为 delayed/probationary admission：boundary-risk candidate 不立即成为长期静态 MapPoint，而是需要跨帧静态支持、足够 local inlier support 或低残差确认后再 promotion。
```

### 4. D²MA-DA-lite 初步原型结果补充

在准备回传前，我们继续实现了一个最小 D²MA-DA-lite 原型：boundary-risk candidate 不再无条件 hard veto，而是要求其邻域内有足够“干净静态已跟踪 MapPoint”作为支持。

实现分为两层：

```text
CKF layer:
  CreateNewKeyFrame 中 RGB-D 单帧深度生成新 MapPoint。

LM layer:
  LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints 中关键帧间三角化生成新 MapPoint。
```

新增开关：

```text
STSLAM_DYNAMIC_MAP_ADMISSION_DELAYED_BOUNDARY
STSLAM_DYNAMIC_MAP_ADMISSION_DELAYED_BOUNDARY_CREATE_NEW_KEYFRAME
STSLAM_DYNAMIC_MAP_ADMISSION_DELAYED_BOUNDARY_LOCAL_MAPPING_CREATE_NEW_MAPPOINTS
STSLAM_DYNAMIC_MAP_ADMISSION_DELAYED_BOUNDARY_SUPPORT_RADIUS_PX
STSLAM_DYNAMIC_MAP_ADMISSION_DELAYED_BOUNDARY_MIN_SUPPORT
STSLAM_DYNAMIC_MAP_ADMISSION_DELAYED_BOUNDARY_MIN_OBS
```

结果文件：

```text
/home/lj/d-drive/Obsidian Vault/小论文/小论文2 动态改进Orb SLAM3/d2ma_da_layered_ablation_summary_20260513.csv
```

结果表：

| sequence | method | matched | ATE-SE3 | ATE-Sim3 | Sim3 scale | RPEt | RPER | final KFs | final MPs |
|---|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| walking_rpy | D²MA-B r5 current ref | 906 | 0.307193 | 0.151482 | 0.275739 | 0.015342 | 0.560025 | 285 | 7393 |
| walking_rpy | D²MA-DA full CKF+LM s18 m2 | 906 | 0.322344 | 0.155957 | 0.251413 | 0.016584 | 0.562662 | 292 | - |
| walking_rpy | D²MA-DA full CKF+LM s18 m3 | 906 | 0.383317 | 0.149283 | 0.229141 | 0.025114 | 0.668378 | 306 | 8067 |
| walking_rpy | D²MA-DA LM-only s18 m2 | 906 | 0.256534 | 0.143501 | 0.346450 | 0.017301 | 0.571184 | 261 | 7180 |
| walking_halfsphere | D²MA-B r5 current ref | 1064 | 0.213132 | 0.168231 | 0.777055 | 0.012444 | 0.451372 | 227 | 5582 |
| walking_halfsphere | D²MA-DA LM-only s18 m2 | 1064 | 0.333637 | 0.238661 | 0.644955 | 0.012844 | 0.464440 | 242 | 5788 |
| walking_halfsphere | D²MA-DA LM-only s18 m3 | 1064 | 0.386641 | 0.263878 | 0.590959 | 0.013968 | 0.468541 | 258 | 6221 |

关键计数：

| sequence | method | CKF skipped new | CKF promoted new | LM rejected boundary pairs | LM promoted boundary pairs |
|---|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|
| walking_rpy | D²MA-B r5 current ref | 9470 | 0 | 298 | 0 |
| walking_rpy | D²MA-DA full CKF+LM s18 m2 | 7022 | 2067 | 223 | 39 |
| walking_rpy | D²MA-DA full CKF+LM s18 m3 | 7856 | 1372 | 232 | 15 |
| walking_rpy | D²MA-DA LM-only s18 m2 | 9444 | 0 | 310 | 74 |
| walking_halfsphere | D²MA-B r5 current ref | 11183 | 0 | 397 | 0 |
| walking_halfsphere | D²MA-DA LM-only s18 m2 | 11141 | 0 | 317 | 59 |
| walking_halfsphere | D²MA-DA LM-only s18 m3 | 11237 | 0 | 356 | 47 |

初步解读：

- full CKF+LM DA 不理想，尤其 CKF 层会把大量单帧 RGB-D boundary new MapPoint 放回静态地图：`m2` 放回 2067 个，`m3` 仍放回 1372 个，导致 `walking_rpy` 全局尺度/SE3 退化。
- LM-only DA 在 `walking_rpy` 上优于当前 hard D²MA-B reference：ATE-SE3 `0.307193 -> 0.256534`，ATE-Sim3 `0.151482 -> 0.143501`，scale `0.275739 -> 0.346450`。
- 但同样的 LM-only DA 在 `walking_halfsphere` 上明显退化：ATE-SE3 `0.213132 -> 0.333637`，scale `0.777055 -> 0.644955`；提高 `min_support=3` 仍不能救回。
- 这说明 D²MA-DA 不宜作为默认替代 D²MA-B 的固定模块，而更像一个 conditional/local recovery module：只应在特定 failure mode 下、只在 LocalMapping 几何准入层、以很小 budget 放行 support-confirmed boundary pairs。

### 5. 请重点回答

1. 现在是否可以把 D²MA-B r5 正式作为论文主方法，而 D²MA-min 作为核心消融？
2. same-count non-boundary control + `walking_halfsphere` 外部验证是否足够支撑 “不是泛化删点，而是 targeted boundary-risk map admission”？
3. 基于 D²MA-DA-lite 的正负结果，你是否建议将 D²MA-DA 定位为 conditional/local recovery module，而不是默认主方法？
4. 如果继续实现 adaptive D²MA-DA，触发条件应该优先用什么：local inlier margin、tracked static support、scale/path proxy、boundary admission budget，还是 failure-frame detector？
5. 论文中如何表述 D²MA-B 与 D²MA-DA 的关系：D²MA-B 作为主方法，D²MA-DA 作为机制扩展/失败边界讨论，还是两个阶段的统一框架？

## 答
According to a document from 2026-05-13, my updated judgment is: **yes, the paper mainline can now formally converge to D²MA-min + D²MA-Boundary r5, with D²MA-B r5 as the main method and D²MA-min as the core mechanism ablation.** The same-count non-boundary control and `fr3/walking_halfsphere` validation are exactly the two pieces that were missing to defend the claim that D²MA-B is not just “delete more points,” but **targeted boundary-risk static-map admission control**.

### 1. Main conclusion

You can now write the method stack as:

```text
D²MA-min:
  direct dynamic-depth / instance-bound feature observations are not admitted
  into the persistent static map.

D²MA-B r5:
  D²MA-min
  + boundary-risk admission guard for near-mask RGB-D observations,
    targeting mixed-depth / occlusion-edge / segmentation-boundary leakage.

D²MA-DA:
  not the default main method yet;
  conditional delayed-admission extension for selected residual failure modes.
```

The current evidence is strong enough to make **D²MA-B r5** the primary reported method. D²MA-min remains essential, but as an ablation that proves the core dynamic-depth admission mechanism.

The reason is simple: D²MA-min already proves that direct dynamic-depth map admission is harmful; D²MA-B r5 now proves that **near-mask boundary observations are a second real contamination channel**, not merely a hyperparameter trick.

### 2. Does same-count control prove D²MA-B is not generic sparsification?

Yes, this is now one of your strongest ablations.

On `walking_rpy`, D²MA-B r5 improves from D²MA-min’s `ATE-SE3=0.367386`, `scale=0.260907`, `final KFs/MPs=426/7331` to `ATE-SE3=0.269999`, `scale=0.361678`, `final KFs/MPs=370/6006`. The same-count non-boundary control deletes almost the same number of candidates, but gives `ATE-SE3=0.604425`, `scale=0.138884`, `final KFs/MPs=427/7389`, which is worse than D²MA-min and far worse than D²MA-B r5. The control also matches the boundary budget closely: `7990` boundary new-candidate budget vs `7988` skipped non-boundary new candidates, and `246` boundary LM-pair budget vs `209` skipped non-boundary LM pairs.

That supports a clean claim:

> D²MA-B’s benefit is not caused by reducing the number of MapPoints or making the map sparser. It comes from vetoing a specific high-risk class: static-labeled observations near dynamic-mask boundaries.

This is much more defensible than “we dilate the mask by 5 px.” You should avoid the dilation wording and instead call it:

```text
boundary-risk map admission control
```

or:

```text
near-dynamic-boundary depth provenance guard
```

### 3. Does `walking_halfsphere` support external generalization?

Yes, and it supports the main story better than `walking_rpy` alone.

For `fr3/walking_halfsphere`, the raw RGB-D baseline has `ATE-SE3=0.418817`, `scale=0.560136`, `final KFs/MPs=610/13213`. D²MA-min improves it to `ATE-SE3=0.178466`, `scale=0.798252`, `final KFs/MPs=370/5491`; D²MA-B r5 further improves it to `ATE-SE3=0.156093`, `scale=0.823258`, `final KFs/MPs=308/4804`. RPE also improves monotonically: `RPEt=0.020018 -> 0.016987 -> 0.016220`, and `RPER=0.521662 -> 0.498543 -> 0.484402`.

This matters because `walking_halfsphere` is not just another run of `walking_xyz`. It is a different dynamic motion sequence with 1067 exported frames and a mean mask ratio of `0.129538`; the same association policy is used for all compared methods, even though the raw association has some timestamp mismatches.

The strongest interpretation is:

> Across multiple TUM dynamic person sequences, D²MA-min reduces dynamic-depth map pollution, and D²MA-B r5 further suppresses boundary-risk leakage. The improvement is not limited to `walking_xyz`.

You should still be cautious: this does not prove universal robustness on all dynamic RGB-D scenes. But it is enough for a small paper route, especially because the trend is consistent in ATE, scale, KFs/MPs, and RPE.

### 4. Should D²MA-B r5 be the main method?

Yes.

Use this hierarchy in the paper:

| Role                | Method              | Purpose                                                 |
| ------------------- | ------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------- |
| Raw baseline        | raw RGB-D ORB-SLAM3 | shows dynamic-depth/map contamination failure           |
| Core ablation       | D²MA-min            | proves direct dynamic-depth admission is harmful        |
| Main method         | D²MA-B r5           | handles direct dynamic-depth plus near-boundary leakage |
| Mechanism extension | D²MA-DA             | explores delayed/probationary admission, not default    |

D²MA-B r5 should be the main method because it is now supported by three distinct findings:

1. It improves `walking_rpy` beyond D²MA-min.
2. It improves `walking_halfsphere` beyond D²MA-min.
3. Same-count non-boundary deletion fails badly, showing boundary targeting matters.

D²MA-min should not be the final main method anymore. It is still important, but its role is now:

> D²MA-min isolates the first-order dynamic-depth static-map admission channel; D²MA-B adds the second-order boundary-risk channel required for broader dynamic-sequence robustness.

### 5. How to position D²MA-DA after the new results?

D²MA-DA should **not** become the default method yet. It should be framed as a conditional / local recovery extension.

Your DA-lite results are mixed in a very informative way. On `walking_rpy`, LM-only DA improves the current hard D²MA-B reference from `ATE-SE3=0.307193`, `scale=0.275739` to `ATE-SE3=0.256534`, `scale=0.346450`. But the same LM-only DA damages `walking_halfsphere`, degrading from `ATE-SE3=0.213132`, `scale=0.777055` to `ATE-SE3=0.333637`, `scale=0.644955`; increasing `min_support=3` does not fix it.

The CKF+LM version is worse: on `walking_rpy`, full DA with CKF+LM re-admits many single-frame RGB-D boundary candidates. The `m2` setting promotes `2067` CKF boundary candidates, and `m3` still promotes `1372`; both degrade the global SE3/scale behavior relative to the better LM-only variant.

So the correct conclusion is:

> Delayed admission is not wrong, but CKF-level delayed admission is currently unsafe. Boundary-risk candidates created from single-frame RGB-D depth should remain hard-vetoed. If delayed admission is used, it should be restricted to LocalMapping triangulation pairs and activated only under diagnosed support-starvation or residual-failure conditions.

This is important: **DA is not a replacement for D²MA-B; it is a recovery mode for cases where hard boundary veto is too conservative.**

### 6. D²MA-DA minimum implementation route

The next D²MA-DA version should be smaller than what you already tried, not larger.

#### 6.1 Do not promote CKF boundary candidates

Keep this fixed:

```text
CreateNewKeyFrame boundary-risk RGB-D new MapPoint:
  always hard veto under D²MA-B r5
```

Reason: CKF boundary candidates are single-frame depth observations. They are exactly the kind of near-mask mixed-depth measurement that caused the problem. Your full CKF+LM DA already showed that promoting them reintroduces map contamination.

#### 6.2 Only allow LM-layer delayed admission

Allow delayed admission only here:

```text
LocalMapping::CreateNewMapPoints
```

Rationale: LM pairs have at least two-view geometric structure, epipolar consistency, baseline/parallax constraints, descriptor agreement, and later residual checks. They are safer candidates for probationary admission than CKF single-frame RGB-D unprojection.

#### 6.3 Add a tiny global budget

Do not allow arbitrary LM boundary promotions. Your current LM-only DA promoted `74` boundary pairs on `walking_rpy` and improved, but promoted `59` on `walking_halfsphere` and hurt. That suggests even small numbers can be harmful if activated in the wrong context.

A safe first budget:

```text
max_promoted_boundary_lm_pairs_per_keyframe = 1 or 2
max_promoted_boundary_lm_pairs_per_20_keyframes = 10
```

This turns DA into a sparse rescue mechanism, not a general admission policy.

#### 6.4 Require both support and failure context

A boundary LM pair should be promoted only if two conditions hold:

```text
local static support is weak enough that hard-veto may be starving the map
AND
the candidate itself has enough static/geometric support
```

This avoids the `walking_halfsphere` failure mode, where D²MA-B already works well and DA unnecessarily re-admits risky boundary structure.

### 7. Adaptive D²MA-DA trigger priority

Use this priority order:

#### First: tracked static support / static inlier margin

This should be the main trigger.

Define per keyframe or local mapping window:

```text
tracked_static_mps
local_static_inliers
static_inlier_margin = static_inliers - min_required_static_inliers
```

Trigger DA only when:

```text
static_inlier_margin < threshold
or
tracked_static_mps in local window < threshold
```

Why this is better than path/scale proxy: it is online, local, directly tied to ORB-SLAM3 survival, and does not require ground truth.

#### Second: boundary admission budget pressure

Use a ratio like:

```text
boundary_veto_ratio = boundary_skipped_candidates / accepted_static_candidates
```

or:

```text
boundary_lm_reject_count_per_keyframe
```

Trigger DA only if boundary rejection is high **and** static support is weak:

```text
if boundary_reject_high && static_support_low:
    enable LM-only probationary admission
else:
    keep hard D²MA-B r5
```

This prevents DA from activating on `walking_halfsphere` just because some boundary pairs exist.

#### Third: local residual / reprojection quality of the candidate

For a candidate boundary LM pair, require:

```text
low reprojection residual
sufficient parallax
positive depth in both views
descriptor match consistency
not inside dynamic mask in either endpoint
not on direct dynamic instance
near-boundary only, not inside-mask
```

This should be a candidate-level filter, not the global trigger.

#### Fourth: short-horizon path proxy

Use this only as a diagnostic, not the primary online trigger.

A short-horizon path proxy can be useful:

```text
estimated arc length over last N frames
KF translation jump
velocity inconsistency
```

But without GT, it is noisy. It may catch obvious explosions, but it is not as clean as static inlier/support statistics.

#### Avoid: generic failure-frame detector as the main trigger

A black-box failure detector is hard to explain and may be reviewer-hostile. The paper’s strength is mechanistic clarity. Keep triggers tied to SLAM quantities:

```text
static support
boundary veto pressure
candidate geometry quality
promotion budget
```

### 8. Concrete adaptive D²MA-DA logic

A minimal version:

```cpp
// Default: D²MA-B r5 hard-veto.
if (candidate.isDirectDynamic()) {
    veto();
}

if (candidate.isBoundaryRisk()) {
    if (stage == CreateNewKeyFrame) {
        veto();  // never promote single-frame RGB-D boundary depth
    }

    if (stage == LocalMappingCreateNewMapPoints) {
        if (!localStaticSupportLow()) {
            veto();
        }
        if (!boundaryVetoPressureHigh()) {
            veto();
        }
        if (!candidateGeometryStrong(candidate)) {
            veto();
        }
        if (!promotionBudgetAvailable()) {
            veto();
        }

        probationaryAdmit(candidate);
    }
}
```

Candidate geometry checks:

```text
endpoint A and B are outside direct dynamic mask
both endpoints are boundary-risk, not inside-mask
sufficient parallax
low triangulation reprojection error
depth consistency if depth available
descriptor distance below strict threshold
nearby clean static MapPoint support >= k
```

Promotion state:

```text
probationary MapPoint:
  not used in pose optimization immediately, or used with conservative rules
  not counted as stable static support initially
  promoted after >= 2 successful observations outside dynamic mask
  promoted only if residual stays low and it survives normal culling
```

If implementation time is limited, skip explicit MapPoint state and use a stricter one-shot “LM-only conditional admit” first:

```text
D²MA-DA-lite-v2:
  CKF boundary = hard veto
  LM boundary = allow only if:
      static_support_low
      boundary_pressure_high
      candidate_geometry_strong
      per-KF promotion budget not exceeded
```

That is probably the fastest next experiment.

### 9. How to write D²MA-B and D²MA-DA relationship in the paper

Use this framing:

```text
D²MA-B is the proposed main method.
D²MA-DA is an exploratory extension that reveals the limitation of hard boundary veto
and motivates future support-aware admission.
```

Do not present them as a unified two-stage final framework yet. The evidence does not support that, because DA helps `walking_rpy` but hurts `walking_halfsphere`.

A stable paper wording:

> D²MA-B uses a conservative boundary-risk veto as the default admission policy. We additionally investigate a delayed-admission variant that re-admits support-confirmed boundary candidates. The variant improves one residual failure case but degrades another dynamic sequence, indicating that delayed admission should be activated conditionally rather than used as a universal replacement for hard boundary veto.

That wording turns the mixed DA results into a strength: you are not overclaiming; you are mapping the failure boundary of the method.

### 10. Updated paper narrative

The narrative is now ready to converge:

```text
1. Raw RGB-D ORB-SLAM3 in dynamic scenes fails not only because of dynamic features,
   but because dynamic foreground depth is admitted into the persistent static map.

2. D²MA-min blocks direct dynamic-depth static-map admission at CreateNewKeyFrame
   and LocalMapping.

3. External sequences reveal a residual channel:
   static-labeled features near dynamic masks can still carry mixed or boundary depth.

4. D²MA-B r5 adds boundary-risk admission veto.
   It improves both walking_rpy and walking_halfsphere.

5. Same-count non-boundary deletion fails,
   proving that D²MA-B is targeted boundary-risk admission control, not generic sparsification.

6. Delayed admission can recover some over-vetoed boundary structure,
   but current DA-lite is sequence-dependent.
   Therefore, it is a conditional extension, not the main method.
```

This is a coherent small-paper story.

### 11. What to include in the main paper tables

#### Main performance table

Include:

```text
walking_xyz:
  raw RGB-D
  filtered depth C
  D²MA-min
  D²MA-B r5

walking_rpy:
  raw RGB-D
  D²MA-min
  D²MA-B r5
  same-count non-boundary control

walking_halfsphere:
  raw RGB-D
  D²MA-min
  D²MA-B r5
```

You can include filtered-depth C/D for `walking_rpy` and `walking_halfsphere` if available, but they should be presented as upper-bound / diagnostic, not as your main method.

#### Ablation table

Include:

```text
D²MA-min
D²MA-B r3
D²MA-B r5
D²MA-B r8
same-count non-boundary r5
```

#### DA discussion table

Include:

```text
D²MA-B r5 current ref
D²MA-DA CKF+LM
D²MA-DA LM-only
```

But put DA in an “extension / limitation analysis” section, not in the core method table.

### 12. What remains necessary before submission

#### Must finish

1. Repeat stability for D²MA-B r5 on `walking_halfsphere` if not already done.
2. Repeat stability for same-count non-boundary control on `walking_rpy`, at least one duplicate run.
3. A short qualitative figure showing boundary-risk points near mask edges being vetoed.
4. A table showing D²MA-B does not modify RGB, does not invalidate current-frame depth, and does not reweight pose optimization.
5. Clear disclosure that `walking_halfsphere` has timestamp mismatches, but all compared methods use the same association.

#### Strongly recommended

1. One static / low-dynamic negative control with D²MA-B r5.
2. Runtime split:

   ```text
   foundation model frontend
   D²MA backend overhead
   total pipeline
   ```
3. A map-size / keyframe-inflation plot over time for raw, D²MA-min, D²MA-B.
4. A boundary-risk provenance histogram:

   ```text
   inside dynamic mask
   near-mask boundary
   far static
   accepted / vetoed / promoted
   ```

#### Optional

1. Full delayed/probationary MapPoint state.
2. Additional TUM dynamic sequence.
3. Comparison to DS-SLAM / DynaSLAM if easy to reproduce in the same evaluation protocol.
4. Monocular discussion.

### 13. Final recommendation

The mainline should now be:

> **D²MA-B r5: Dynamic-Depth-Aware Map Admission with Boundary-Risk Guard.**

Use D²MA-min as the mechanism ablation. Use same-count non-boundary veto as the key anti-sparsification control. Use `walking_halfsphere` as the external dynamic validation. Keep D²MA-DA as a conditional extension and failure-boundary discussion.

The next implementation step should not be “make DA bigger.” It should be:

```text
Adaptive LM-only D²MA-DA:
  CKF boundary remains hard-vetoed.
  LM boundary candidates may be admitted only when
  static support is low,
  boundary veto pressure is high,
  candidate geometry is strong,
  and a strict promotion budget allows it.
```

That gives you a clean final position: **D²MA-B is the paper method; D²MA-DA is the next research direction for support-aware recovery when conservative boundary veto becomes too restrictive.**

1. 已被当前数据支持的结论

请特别注意：我们已经发现 ORB-SLAM3 全序列结果存在分支漂移，不能只看单次 ATE。请你必须同时检查 matched poses / coverage / final KFs / final MPs / repeat mean-std / negative control，而不是只根据 RMSE 下判断。

### 4. 关键 raw observations

- `walking_rpy` D²MA-B r5 三次中，有一次 matched poses 从 `906` 掉到 `822`，但 ATE-SE3 反而更低到 `0.173807`；这说明短轨迹/丢尾轨迹可能让 ATE 虚假变好。
- `walking_rpy` D²MA-B r5 的另外两次完全一致：matched `906`，ATE-SE3 `0.244055`，scale `0.367900`。
- `walking_rpy` same-count control 也出现 matched `822/906` 两种分支，但两次都明显差于 D²MA-B r5，对照结论仍成立。
- `walking_halfsphere` repeat 很稳定：matched 都是 `1064`，ATE-SE3 `0.215148-0.230147`，scale `0.764877-0.775176`。
- `walking_halfsphere` 当前 repeat mean `0.223301` 明显保守于早期单次 `0.156093`，因此论文主表不应使用早期单次最优。
- `walking_static` 的 SE3/RPE 很稳定，但 Sim3 scale 很低，可能与该低运动/尺度可观测性有关，不应作为主要尺度论据。
- `walking_xyz` 当前 repeat mean ATE-SE3 `0.164883`，明显不如早期记录中的低 ATE，需要判断是否是当前二进制/config/data口径变化，还是该序列本身在当前 D²MA-B r5 下并不强。

### 5. 请严格回答

1. 基于 repeat mean/std，而不是早期单次最好值，D²MA-B r5 是否仍足以作为主方法？
2. `walking_rpy` matched poses 漂移如何在论文中处理？是否需要把 matched=822 的 run 标记为 tracking truncation/failure branch，而不是和完整 run 直接平均？
3. 主表应该用 mean/std、median/IQR，还是 coverage-filtered mean？例如是否只统计 matched poses 等于完整 coverage 的 run？
4. same-count control 的负对照是否仍足够强？还需要补第 3 次 repeat 吗？
5. `walking_halfsphere` 早期单次 `0.156093` 与 repeat mean `0.223301` 不一致，应如何诚实写？是否必须放弃旧单次结果？
6. `walking_static` 的低 Sim3 scale 是否会削弱论证？它应该作为 negative control、sanity check，还是不放主表？
7. `walking_xyz` 当前 repeat 表现较差，是否说明 D²MA-B r5 还需要回头检查 config/data口径？还是可以把它作为困难/不稳定序列处理？
8. 在当前证据下，一篇小论文最稳的主张应该怎么收敛，避免过度声称？
9. 请列出“必须补”的最小实验清单，按优先级排序，并说明每个实验若失败会如何改变论文主线。
10. 请给出最终论文表格设计：主表、消融表、负对照表、可复现性表分别放什么，不要混用旧/新二进制结果。

请用严格、可执行的方式回答；如果某些结论不能判断，请直接说“不能判断，需要补实验”，不要为了完整性强行给建议。
